\\n8: # API semantic versioning\\n9: \\n10: The Envoy APIs consist of a family of packages, e.g. `envoy.admin.v3alpha`,\\n11: `envoy.service.trace.v3`. Each package is independently versioned with a protobuf semantic\\n12: versioning scheme based on https://cloud.google.com/apis/design/versioning.\\n13: \\n14: The major version for a package is captured in its name (and directory structure). Each package is independently versioned with a protobuf semantic\n12: versioning scheme based on https://cloud.google.com/apis/design/versioning.\n13: \n14: The major version for a package is captured in its name (and directory structure).
